                         {
                              "title": "团队如何统一代码规范？",
                              "description": "## 一、 集成editorconfig配置\r\n\r\nEditorConfig 有助于为不同 IDE 编辑器上处理同一项目的多个开发人员维护一致的编码风格。\r\n\r\n根目录下创建.editorconfig文件，其内容如下：\r\n```javascript\r\n# http://editorconfig.org\r\n\r\nroot = true\r\n\r\n[*] # 表示所有文件适用\r\ncharset = utf-8 # 设置文件字符集为 utf-8\r\nindent_style = space # 缩进风格（tab | space）\r\nindent_size = 2 # 缩进大小\r\nend_of_line = lf # 控制换行类型(lf | cr | crlf)\r\ntrim_trailing_whitespace = true # 去除行首的任意空白字符\r\ninsert_final_newline = true # 始终在文件末尾插入一个新行\r\n\r\n[*.md] # 表示仅 md 文件适用以下规则\r\nmax_line_length = off\r\ntrim_trailing_whitespace = false\r\n```\r\n\r\nVSCode需要安装一个插件：EditorConfig for VS Code,webstrom就不需要了！\r\n\r\n![image-20210722215138665](https://tva1.sinaimg.cn/large/008i3skNgy1gsq2gh989yj30pj05ggmb.jpg)\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n## 二、 使用prettier工具\r\n\r\nPrettier 是一款强大的代码格式化工具，支持 JavaScript、TypeScript、CSS、SCSS、Less、JSX、Angular、Vue、GraphQL、JSON、Markdown 等语言，基本上前端能用到的文件格式它都可以搞定，是当下最流行的代码格式化工具。\r\n\r\n1.安装prettier\r\n\r\n```shell\r\nnpm install prettier -D\r\n```\r\n\r\n2.配置.prettierrc文件：\r\n\r\n* useTabs：使用tab缩进还是空格缩进，选择false；\r\n* tabWidth：tab是空格的情况下，是几个空格，选择2个；\r\n* printWidth：当行字符的长度，推荐80，也有人喜欢100或者120；\r\n* singleQuote：使用单引号还是双引号，选择true，使用单引号；\r\n* trailingComma：在多行输入的尾逗号是否添加，设置为 `none`；\r\n* semi：语句末尾是否要加分号，默认值true，选择false表示不加；\r\n\r\n```json\r\n{\r\n  \"useTabs\": false,\r\n  \"tabWidth\": 2,\r\n  \"printWidth\": 80,\r\n  \"singleQuote\": true,\r\n  \"trailingComma\": \"none\",\r\n  \"semi\": false\r\n}\r\n```\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n3.创建.prettierignore忽略文件\r\n\r\n```\r\n/dist/*\r\n.local\r\n.output.js\r\n/node_modules/**\r\n\r\n**/*.svg\r\n**/*.sh\r\n\r\n/public/*\r\n```\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n4.VSCode需要安装prettier的插件\r\n\r\n![image-20210722214543454](https://tva1.sinaimg.cn/large/008i3skNgy1gsq2acx21rj30ow057mxp.jpg)\r\n\r\n5.测试prettier是否生效\r\n\r\n* 测试一：在代码中保存代码；\r\n* 测试二：配置一次性修改的命令；\r\n\r\n在package.json中配置一个scripts：\r\n\r\n```json\r\n    \"prettier\": \"prettier --write .\"\r\n```\r\n于是执行命令行`npm run prettier` 便可以将项目中所有代码格式化。\r\n\r\n\r\n## 三、 使用ESLint检测\r\n\r\n1.在前面创建项目的时候，我们就选择了ESLint，所以Vue会默认帮助我们配置需要的ESLint环境。\r\n\r\n2.VSCode需要安装ESLint插件：\r\n\r\n![image-20210722215933360](https://tva1.sinaimg.cn/large/008i3skNgy1gsq2oq26odj30pw05faaq.jpg)\r\n\r\n3.解决eslint和prettier冲突的问题：\r\n\r\n安装插件：（vue在创建项目时，如果选择prettier，那么这两个插件会自动安装）\r\n\r\n```shell\r\nnpm i eslint-plugin-prettier eslint-config-prettier -D\r\n```\r\n\r\n然后在.eslintrc.js文件中添加以下配置： \r\n\r\n```js\r\n  extends: [\r\n    \"plugin:vue/vue3-essential\",\r\n    \"eslint:recommended\",\r\n    \"@vue/typescript/recommended\",\r\n    \"@vue/prettier\",\r\n    \"@vue/prettier/@typescript-eslint\",\r\n    'plugin:prettier/recommended'\r\n  ],\r\n```\r\n最后在vscode 设置中，将下面这一项打勾\r\n![image](https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/36322912/174449723-dce043ae-7366-4002-a415-b929d83ed785.png)\r\n\r\n于是当我们保存代码时候，就能生成符合eslint规范的格式化代码。\r\n\r\n## 四、 git Husky和eslint\r\n\r\n虽然我们已经要求项目使用eslint了，但是不能保证组员提交代码之前都将eslint中的问题解决掉了：\r\n\r\n* 也就是我们希望保证代码仓库中的代码都是符合eslint规范的；\r\n\r\n* 那么我们需要在组员执行 `git commit ` 命令的时候对其进行校验，如果不符合eslint规范，那么自动通过规范进行修复；\r\n\r\n那么如何做到这一点呢？可以通过Husky工具：\r\n\r\n* husky是一个git hook工具，可以帮助我们触发git提交的各个阶段：pre-commit、commit-msg、pre-push\r\n\r\n如何使用husky呢？\r\n\r\n这里我们可以使用自动配置命令：\r\n\r\n```shell\r\nnpx husky-init && npm install\r\n```\r\n\r\n这里会做三件事：\r\n\r\n1.安装husky相关的依赖：\r\n\r\n![image-20210723112648927](https://tva1.sinaimg.cn/large/008i3skNgy1gsqq0o5jxmj30bb04qwen.jpg)\r\n\r\n2.在项目目录下创建 `.husky` 文件夹：\r\n\r\n```\r\nnpx huksy install\r\n```\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n![image-20210723112719634](https://tva1.sinaimg.cn/large/008i3skNgy1gsqq16zo75j307703mt8m.jpg)\r\n\r\n3.在package.json中添加一个脚本：\r\n\r\n![image-20210723112817691](https://tva1.sinaimg.cn/large/008i3skNgy1gsqq26phpxj30dj06fgm3.jpg)\r\n\r\n接下来，我们需要去完成一个操作：在进行commit时，执行lint脚本：\r\n\r\n![image-20210723112932943](https://tva1.sinaimg.cn/large/008i3skNgy1gsqq3hn229j30nf04z74q.jpg)\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n这个时候我们执行git commit的时候会自动对代码进行lint校验。\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n## 五、 git commit规范\r\n\r\n### 1. 代码提交风格\r\n\r\n通常我们的git commit会按照统一的风格来提交，这样可以快速定位每次提交的内容，方便之后对版本进行控制。\r\n\r\n![](https://tva1.sinaimg.cn/large/008i3skNgy1gsqw17gaqjj30to0cj3zp.jpg)\r\n\r\n但是如果每次手动来编写这些是比较麻烦的事情，我们可以使用一个工具：Commitizen\r\n\r\n* Commitizen 是一个帮助我们编写规范 commit message 的工具；\r\n\r\n1.安装Commitizen\r\n\r\n```shell\r\nnpm install commitizen -D\r\n```\r\n\r\n2.安装cz-conventional-changelog，并且初始化cz-conventional-changelog：\r\n\r\n```shell\r\nnpx commitizen init cz-conventional-changelog --save-dev --save-exact\r\n```\r\n\r\n这个命令会帮助我们安装cz-conventional-changelog：\r\n\r\n![image-20210723145249096](https://tva1.sinaimg.cn/large/008i3skNgy1gsqvz2odi4j30ek00zmx2.jpg)\r\n\r\n并且在package.json中进行配置：\r\n\r\n![](https://tva1.sinaimg.cn/large/008i3skNgy1gsqvzftay5j30iu04k74d.jpg)\r\n\r\n这个时候我们提交代码需要使用 `npx cz`：\r\n\r\n* 第一步是选择type，本次更新的类型\r\n\r\n| Type     | 作用                                                         |\r\n| -------- | ------------------------------------------------------------ |\r\n| feat     | 新增特性 (feature)                                           |\r\n| fix      | 修复 Bug(bug fix)                                            |\r\n| docs     | 修改文档 (documentation)                                     |\r\n| style    | 代码格式修改(white-space, formatting, missing semi colons, etc) |\r\n| refactor | 代码重构(refactor)                                           |\r\n| perf     | 改善性能(A code change that improves performance)            |\r\n| test     | 测试(when adding missing tests)                              |\r\n| build    | 变更项目构建或外部依赖（例如 scopes: webpack、gulp、npm 等） |\r\n| ci       | 更改持续集成软件的配置文件和 package 中的 scripts 命令，例如 scopes: Travis, Circle 等 |\r\n| chore    | 变更构建流程或辅助工具(比如更改测试环境)                     |\r\n| revert   | 代码回退                                                     |\r\n\r\n* 第二步选择本次修改的范围（作用域）\r\n\r\n![image-20210723150147510](https://tva1.sinaimg.cn/large/008i3skNgy1gsqw8ca15oj30r600wmx4.jpg)\r\n\r\n* 第三步选择提交的信息\r\n\r\n![image-20210723150204780](https://tva1.sinaimg.cn/large/008i3skNgy1gsqw8mq3zlj60ni01hmx402.jpg)\r\n\r\n* 第四步提交详细的描述信息\r\n\r\n![image-20210723150223287](https://tva1.sinaimg.cn/large/008i3skNgy1gsqw8y05bjj30kt01fjrb.jpg)\r\n\r\n* 第五步是否是一次重大的更改\r\n\r\n![image-20210723150322122](https://tva1.sinaimg.cn/large/008i3skNgy1gsqw9z5vbij30bm00q744.jpg)\r\n\r\n* 第六步是否影响某个open issue\r\n\r\n![image-20210723150407822](https://tva1.sinaimg.cn/large/008i3skNgy1gsqwar8xp1j30fq00ya9x.jpg)\r\n\r\n我们也可以在scripts中构建一个命令来执行 cz：\r\n\r\n![image-20210723150526211](https://tva1.sinaimg.cn/large/008i3skNgy1gsqwc4gtkxj30e207174t.jpg)\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n### 2.  代码提交验证\r\n\r\n如果我们按照cz来规范了提交风格，但是依然有同事通过 `git commit` 按照不规范的格式提交应该怎么办呢？\r\n\r\n* 我们可以通过commitlint来限制提交；\r\n\r\n1.安装 @commitlint/config-conventional 和 @commitlint/cli\r\n\r\n```shell\r\nnpm i @commitlint/config-conventional @commitlint/cli -D\r\n```\r\n\r\n2.在根目录创建commitlint.config.js文件，配置commitlint\r\n\r\n```js\r\nmodule.exports = {\r\n  extends: ['@commitlint/config-conventional']\r\n}\r\n```\r\n\r\n3.使用husky生成commit-msg文件，验证提交信息：\r\n\r\n```shell\r\nnpx husky add .husky/commit-msg \"npx --no-install commitlint --edit $1\"\r\n```\r\n",

                              "title": "如何在线预览 GitHub 项目",
                              "description": "![本文框架图](https://user-gold-cdn.xitu.io/2018/5/30/163b041962eff842?w=959&h=735&f=png&s=74961)\r\n\r\n## 一、Git是什么，它与Github什么关系\r\n\r\nGit是一款免费、开源的分布式源代码管理工具。\r\nGithub是用Git做版本控制的代码托管平台。\r\n## 二、Git常用命令\r\n\r\n![](https://user-gold-cdn.xitu.io/2018/5/30/163b041962d95f3c?w=617&h=181&f=png&s=70289)\r\n\r\n一般来说，Git命令日常使用只要记住上图6个命令，就可以了。但是熟练使用，恐怕要记住60～100个命令。\r\n\r\n接下来归纳了一些常用的命令：\r\n\r\n把普通目录变为git工作区\r\n`$ git init`\r\n\r\n添加当前目录的所有文件到暂存区\r\n`$ git add .`  \r\n\r\n提交暂存区到仓库区\r\n`$ git commit -m “XXX” `\r\n\r\n恢复暂存区的指定文件到工作区\r\n`$ git checkout [file]`\r\ncheckout命令用于从历史提交（或者暂存区域）中拷贝文件到工作目录，也可用于切换分支。\r\n\r\n上传本地指定分支到远程仓库（master分支）\r\n`$ git push origin master`\r\n\r\n取回远程仓库的变化，并与本地分支合并\r\n`$ git pull [remote] [branch]`\r\n\r\n列出所有本地分支\r\n`$ git branch` \r\n\r\n新建一个分支，但依然停留在当前分支\r\n`$ git branch [branch-name]`//比如`git branch dev`创建“dev\"分支\r\n\r\n新建一个分支，并切换到该分支\r\n`$ git checkout -b [branch]`  //比如`git checkout -b dev`切换到“dev\"分支\r\n\r\n合并指定分支到当前分支\r\n`$ git merge [branch]`\r\n\r\n## 三、如何进行多人协作（分支创建与合并）\r\n\r\n#### 1.什么是分支？\r\n分支是为了将修改记录的整体流程分叉保存。分叉后的分支不受其他分支的影响，所以在同一个数据库里可以同时进行多个修改。\r\n#### 2.为什么要创建分支？\r\n为了不受其他开发人员的影响，您可以在主分支上建立自己专用的分支。完成工作后，将自己分支上的修改合并到主分支。常常适用于当前开发的项目新增功能时，**代码还未写完或者出现bug未调试好**，这时创建分支将有效提高工作效率。因为每一次提交的历史记录都会在创建分支保存，所以当发生问题时，定位和修改造成问题的提交就容易多了。\r\n#### 3.如何创建分支以及合并分支？\r\n```\r\ngit checkout -b dev//新建一个分支，并切换到该分支\r\ngit branch//列出所有本地分支:*dev master,并显示当前停留在dev分支上 \r\nvi(m) a.js//在分支上修改文件，然后再上传远程仓库\r\ngit add.\r\ngit commit -m \"update part2\"\r\ngit push origin dev//上传到dev分支远程，接下去要合并分支\r\ngit checkout master//合并分支之前必须在master上\r\ngit pull origin master//在当前master上同步到最新版本\r\ngit merge dev//合并分支\r\ngit push origin master//重新提交到远程仓库\r\n```\r\n![分支创建与合并](https://user-gold-cdn.xitu.io/2018/5/30/163b04196497c8c9?w=490&h=225&f=png&s=64263)\r\n\r\n## 四、如何用Github的gh-pages分支展示自己的项目\r\n\r\n**master分支仅是浏览代码，而无法将页面直接在网页打开，而gh-pages分支则是用于直接浏览源码页面的分支**。当我们写项目的时候，需要部署一个预览页面，就可以采用github的gh-pages分支制作GitHub Pages。\r\n接下来举个例子：如何将我的电脑上“在线教育页面作品”上传到GitHub，并实现在线预览\r\ngit安装完成后，首先配置信息\r\n```\r\n配置用户名：  git config --global user.name \"用户名\"\r\n配置邮箱： git config--global user.email \"邮箱地址\"\r\n查看配置信息： git config --list\r\n```\r\n#### 1.先将作品上传到master分支上\r\n```\r\ngit init //把目标文件夹变为git工作区\r\n```\r\n![](https://user-gold-cdn.xitu.io/2018/5/30/163b041964facc87?w=771&h=349&f=png&s=34069)\r\n```\r\ngit add .\r\ngit commit -m \"education\"\r\n```\r\n接下来创建education仓库，如下图\r\n\r\n![创建仓库](https://user-gold-cdn.xitu.io/2018/5/30/163b041964d53334?w=775&h=520&f=png&s=51335)\r\n\r\n创建好仓库后，页面自动跳转到如下页面：\r\n\r\n![创建好仓库后](https://user-gold-cdn.xitu.io/2018/5/30/163b041965518a78?w=633&h=514&f=png&s=59602)\r\n\r\n接下来输入以下两行命令行:\r\n```\r\ngit remote add origin https://github.com/ljianshu/education.git\r\ngit push -u origin master\r\n```\r\n输入两行命令行后，按提示输入账户密码，如下图：\r\n\r\n![image.png](https://user-gold-cdn.xitu.io/2018/5/30/163b041999eca404?w=684&h=338&f=png&s=23077)\r\n\r\n出现如下页面，意味着文件已经全部上传到master分支上，此时你也可以添加一个README.md文件，便于让他人看懂你上传文件。\r\n\r\n![成功上传到master](https://user-gold-cdn.xitu.io/2018/5/30/163b041998ab6e7f?w=1106&h=429&f=png&s=43826)\r\n\r\n#### 2.创建gh-pages分支,再将作品重新上传到该分支上\r\n```\r\ngit checkout -b gh-pages\r\ngit push -u origin gh-pages\r\n ```   \r\n![gh-pages分支](https://user-gold-cdn.xitu.io/2018/5/30/163b04199becb952?w=1107&h=500&f=png&s=50743)\r\n\r\n那这时候，我们看到已经多出了一个gh-pages分支，那么作品展示地址就是**Github用户名.github.io/创建的仓库名**。本例子线上预览`https://ljianshu.github.io/education`。当然你也可以购买一个特色域名，并且绑定在GitHub服务器上。\r\n#### 3.master修改后如何自动同步到gh-pages分支\r\n每次当作品发生更改变动后，要先提交到master分支然后切换到gh-pages分支又重新提交一次，显然这个过程非常繁琐。接下我们介绍一种方法，只需提交到master分支即可，gh-pages分支无需重新提交，就可实现在线预览：\r\n**打开github项目文件的根目录，先找到.git 这个文件夹（文件夹默认是隐藏的），然后找到config这个文件，并打开该文件，在文件里加入以下两句代码即可：**\r\n```\r\npush = +refs/heads/master:refs/heads/gh-pages\r\npush = +refs/heads/master:refs/heads/master\r\n```\r\n![config](https://user-gold-cdn.xitu.io/2018/5/30/163b0419ad5fc777?w=501&h=466&f=png&s=52556)\r\n\r\n## 五、Hexo+Github搭建自己个人博客\r\n\r\nHexo 是一个基于 Node.js 的快速、简洁且高效的博客框架，可以方便的生成静态网页托管在github和Heroku上。Hexo 因其界面简洁、美观且对各类人群（不只是程序猿）友好而广受欢迎，声望不亚于大名鼎鼎的WordPress。\r\n它有以下几个特点：\r\n- 超快速度----Node.js 所带来的超快生成速度，让上百个页面在几秒内瞬间完成渲染。\r\n- 一键部署----只需一条指令即可部署到 GitHub Pages, Heroku 或其他网站。\r\n- 支持 Markdown----Hexo 支持 GitHub Flavored Markdown 的所有功能，甚至可以整合 Octopress 的大多数插件。\r\n- 丰富的插件----Hexo 拥有强大的插件系统，安装插件可以让 Hexo 支持 Jade, CoffeeScript。\r\n\r\n具体实践操作可以查看官网[Hexo](https://hexo.io/zh-cn/index.html)，以后关于这个主题会更新一篇，敬请关注！",

                         {
                              "title": "BUG: Nested fibers, callback invocation in try block",
                              "description": "Hello,\nthanks for this great library. I have found a interesting issue with it.  I totally understand that it might not be a good idea to place callback invocations inside a `try` block, because then you might catch exceptions you never intended to. But anyway, we are not using try catch blocks in pure node.js. But in `wait.for` we are, so we have to be careful about it.\n\nHere is short example in pure node.js style:\n\n``` javascript\nfunction inner(callback) {\n    try {\n        callback(null);\n    }\n    catch(error) {\n        console.log('inner catch', error);\n        callback(error);\n    }\n}\n\ninner(function(err) {\n    console.log('handler '+err);\n    throw new Error('I wish I am not caught.');\n});\n```\n\n```\nhandler null\ninner catch [Error: I wish I am not caught.]\nhandler Error: I wish I am not caught.\n--- uncaught exception ... ---\n```\n\nThe exception is caught in the try block and this invokes the callback again. When the exception is thrown for the second time the callback invocation is no longer in the try block and we end up with uncaught exception as expected.\n\nSo how does this relates to wait.for? Let's try...\n\n``` javascript\nvar wait = require('wait.for');\n\nfunction inner(callback) {\n    wait.launchFiber(function() {\n        console.log('Inner fiber starting...');\n        try {\n            wait.for(setImmediate);\n            callback(null);\n        }\n        catch (e) {\n            console.log('Inner - catch', e);\n            callback(e);\n            return;\n        }\n        //callback (null); // Works fine - Error is no longer in the inner try block\n    });\n}\n\nwait.launchFiber(function() {\n    console.log('Outer fiber starting...');\n    wait.for(inner);\n    throw new Error('I wish I am not caught.');\n});\n```\n\n```\nOuter fiber starting...\nInner fiber starting...\nInner - catch [Error: I wish I am not caught.]\nOuter fiber starting...\nInner fiber starting...\nInner - catch [Error: I wish I am not caught.]\nOuter fiber starting...\nInner fiber starting...\nInner - catch [Error: I wish I am not caught.]\n.... repeats for ever\n```\n\nAgain, the exception is caught, which is not surprising. The problem starts when the callback is invoked for the second time - the whole outer fiber is restarted! And then the exception is thrown again....\n\nI have spent several hours debugging my code and this is the minimal example where it works. If you put away the inner fiber or `wait.for(setImmediate);` it works as it should - no strange restarts.\n\nI am just guessing - wait.for can't find the correct resume callback any more so it goes back to the beginning of the whole fiber. It should throw an error instead.\n",

                              "title": "forEach canceling source observable",
                              "description": "Hey @jhusain, I was trying to work through a couple more transpile cases and ran into some issues.\n\nHeres a pretty basic synchronous number generator and a simple `take()` function.\n\n``` js\nfunction* nums() {\n  for (var n = 0; ; n++) {\n    yield n;\n  }\n}\n\nfunction take(generator, count) {\n  var i = 1,\n    ary = [];\n\n  for (var value of generator) {\n    ary.push(value);\n\n    if (i >= count) {\n      return ary;\n    }\n    i++;\n  }\n}\n\nvar n = nums();\ntake(n, 3) // => [0, 1, 2]\ntake(n, 3) // => [3, 4, 5]\n```\n\nI'd assume that sprinkling magic `async`s, `await`s and `for on` all over should perverse the same behavior.\n\n``` js\nasync function* nums() {\n  for (var n = 0; ; n++) {\n    yield n;\n  }\n}\n\nasync function take(generator, count) {\n  var i = 1,\n    ary = [];\n\n  for (var value on generator) {\n    ary.push(value);\n\n    if (i >= count) {\n      return ary;\n    }\n    i++;\n  }\n}\n\nvar n = nums();\nawait take(n, 3) // => [0, 1, 2]\nawait take(n, 3) // => [3, 4, 5]\n```\n\nI tried to think through what the transpiled output would be and got stuck.\n\n``` js\nfunction take(generator, count) {\n  var i = 1,\n    ary = [];\n\n  // for...on is supposed to become forEach\n  // forEach will return a Promise when the observer is \"done\"\n  return generator.forEach(function(value) {\n    ary.push(value);\n\n    if (i >= count) {\n      // So it seems this.return will cancel our generator observer completely.\n      // Thats bad since the next time we call `take` the observer is done won't\n      // emit more values.\n      //\n      // Also, our `ary` gets set as `generator`'s return value rather than this\n      // forEach.\n      return this.return(ary);\n    }\n    i++;\n  });\n}\n```\n\nI'm assuming I'm just doing the transpile incorrectly or maybe theres just a bug in the current library code.\n\nThanks again!\n",

                         {
                              "title": "Already existing: Hybrids",
                              "description": "Hi. I wanted this thing before 2 years or so. So I created https://github.com/hybridables/hybridify and called all of them Hybrids, so @hybridables org was created. Last year I spent a lot of time on minimizing and minimizing and decoupling the things - so the smallest thing is `relike`. The master as you see it now isn't the `1.0.9` version which is too old. I'm just working on another underling libs.\n\nCheckout these:\n- [relike](https://github.com/hybridables/relike) - kinda \"promisify\", but no so, because it can be used to create promisify functions/libs. Its signature is `relike(fn, ..args)` which args will be passed to the fn, and returns promise. It also handles \"promisify\"-ing sync functions out of the box.\n- [letta](https://github.com/hybridables/letta) - built on top of `relike`, but it can also accept generator functions. Also handles the `uncaughtException` and `unhandledRejection` events, which `relike` not doing, so using `relike` apps would crash directly on errors like `ENOENT` for example. It also pass all the `co@4` tests, of course integrated for the `relike`s signature.\n- [handle-callback](https://github.com/hybridables/handle-callback), [then-callback](https://github.com/hybridables/then-callback), [handle-arguments](https://github.com/hybridables/handle-arguments) and [is-async-function](https://github.com/tunnckoCore/is-async-function) are ones in the absolute core. Mainly `is-async-function` and `is-callback-function` allows us to do all of this crazy things and libs.\n- [native-promise](https://github.com/tunnckocore/native-promise) - Get native `Promise` or falsey value if not available.\n- [native-or-another](https://github.com/tunnckoCore/native-or-another) - Always will expose native Promise if available, otherwise Bluebird **but only if you don't give another promise** module like q or promise or what you want.\n\nThere are tons of tests on all of the hybrids, tons of cases handled. Ton of work was done and a lot of experience was learned. I'm almost to the final line. Most of my work and these ~250 packages is because of the hybrid idea.\n\nBecause of the hybrids all of the [always-*](https://github.com/hybridables?utf8=%E2%9C%93&query=always) was born. They are more real \"promisify\" providing you different signatures. Most of them are a bit outdated currently, but they works.\n\n**edit:** Why all of them? Because we need different signatures for different scenarios. Why not just a `fn.length` to check if function is async or not? Because it's not so easy. It is error prone and have bugs. The `is-async-function` is just an awesome peace of code.\n\nAll of them work on 0.10, defaulting to Bluebird promise or another that you can choose. But also all of them work totally with **native promise** and **always-first** tries to use it if exists.\n\nCheers. :star2: \n",

                              "title": "Use native-or-bluebird promises",
                              "description": "Apparently there are still some issues with V8's implementation of promises (and others):\n1. https://github.com/tj/co/issues/180\n2. https://github.com/promises-aplus/promises-spec/issues/179\n3. https://github.com/then/promise/pull/67\n4. https://github.com/petkaantonov/bluebird/issues/296\n\nSpecifically, the following code quickly blows up with Native Promise implementations (I tried 0.12.7, and 4.1.2 native promises).\n\n``` js\nfunction run(i) {\n    return  new Promise(function(resolve) {\n        setImmediate(resolve);\n    }).then(function () {\n      return i < 99999999 ? run(i + 1) : i;\n    });\n}\nrun(0).then(function (result) {\n  console.log(result);\n});\n```\n\nThis has apparently been fixed in bluebird. I can't find the specific PR, but the above code chugs along (seemingly endlessly) and does not throw when using bluebird. Also, some highly unscientific benchmarking suggests a 2x / 3x performance increase using bluebird (this is echoed by a number of comments I came across on GitHub and SO). \n\nThe `native-or-bluebird` package is really small. It:\n1. Checks for bluebird and returns that if found.\n2. Checks for native and returns that if found.\n3. Throws or returns `undefined` (depending on how you require it).\n",

               "creationDate": "2019-01-30",

                         {
                              "title": "General Improvements",
                              "description": "Hi loup,\r\n\r\nReviewed your code here and there are a few bugs I noticed and a few api changes would resolve those bugs:\r\n\r\n**Suggestion 1**: Api Example\r\nRight now your api is `mousetrapHook(<Array>(handler<object>))`\r\n\r\nHooks should start with `use<Name>` which allows react's linter to kick in to prevent misuse of the hook.\r\n\r\n```javascript\r\n useMousetrap(<Array>(handler<object>))\r\n```\r\n\r\n**Suggestion 2**: Handle key and actions changes and simplify logic\r\nIf your actions or key changes, your hook will not properly update since the first useEffect does not have any variable dependences. Also, having hook depend on arrays is difficult to deal with this challenge. Finally there is no reason to use useState in your hook.\r\n\r\nChange your api to  \r\n```javascript\r\n useMousetrap(<string>key, <fn>action)\r\n```\r\n\r\nAnd your hook to \r\n\r\n```javascript\r\nexport default function useMousetrap = (key, action) => {\r\n\r\n  useEffect(() => {\r\n    mousetrap.bind(keys, action);\r\n    return () =>  mousetrap.unbind(keys);\r\n  }, [key, action]);\r\n}\r\n```\r\n\r\nThe one caveat with any hook is that objects need to be memoized properly otherwise updates to useEffect will constantly change.\r\n\r\nThe the example should utilize reacts's useCallback\r\n\r\n```javascript\r\nconst onCtrlEnter = useCallback(() => {\r\n  \r\n});\r\nuseMousetrap(\"ctrl+enter\", onCtrlEnter);\r\n\r\nconst onCtrlX = useCallback(() => {\r\n  \r\n}) \r\nuseMousetrap(\"ctrl+x\", onCtrlX);\r\n```\r\n\r\n\r\n",

                         {
                              "title": "[Feature Request] Increase usefulness of data-autofill",
                              "description": "First, thanks for making this useful module!\r\n\r\nI'm currently attempting to use `<auto-complete />` inside of a grid where each row contains a single `<auto-complete />`. I assign each `<auto-complete />` a unique id based on its position in the array being iterated to generate the rows. I then use **data-autofill** to populate a hidden input with the actual value, in this case a unique ID, that I need from the AJAX response. This is where I'm having an issue.\r\n\r\nBecause data-autofill uses a name selector, all hidden input values are being updated. A supporting data attribute like the example below would be really useful in cases where multiple `<auto-complete />`'s are used on a single page to fetch similar results. See example below.\r\n\r\n```\r\n<auto-complete api=\"@Request.Path?handler=PlantItemSearch&query=${plantItemDataList_@i}&plantId=@Model.PlantId&fields=plantItemId;itemNumber;itemName\"\r\n    resultname=\"itemNumber\"\r\n    querymin=\"2\"\r\n    optionmax=\"50\"\r\n    inputdelay=\"150\">\r\n        <input type=\"text\" id=\"plantItemDataList_@i\" name=\"plantItemDataList_@i\" autocomplete=\"off\" placeholder=\"Enter Item Name or Number\" value=\"@itemNumber\" />\r\n</auto-complete>\r\n<input type=\"hidden\" \r\n            name=\"@namePrefix.@(nameof(PurchaseOrderDetailAddEdit.PlantItemId))\"\r\n            value=\"@poDetail.PlantItemId\"\r\n            data-autofill=\"plantItemId\"\r\n            data-autofill-source=\"id=\"plantItemDataList_@i\"\" />\r\n```\r\n\r\nAdmittedly, I haven't dug into the complexity of the code, but on the face of it, it seems like `data-autofill-source` could be added as an optional argument simply by updating this selector:\r\n\r\n```\r\nArray.from(this.input.form.querySelectorAll(`[data-autofill=\"${ name }\"]`)).forEach(f => {\r\n    f.value = data[name] || '';\r\n    reset[name] = '';\r\n});\r\n```\r\n\r\nTo this:\r\n\r\n```\r\nArray.from(this.input.form.querySelectorAll(`[data-autofill=\"${name}\"]:not([data-autofill-source]), [data-autofill=\"${name}\"][data-autofill-source=\"${(this.input.name || this.input.id)}\"]`)).forEach(f => {\r\n    f.value = data[name] || '';\r\n    reset[name] = '';\r\n});\r\n```\r\n\r\nAlternatively, exposing a custom change event that includes all fields in the fields query string param could also work, although it seems less elegant. Thoughts?",
